  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer15785601057483061866"><i>Librarian's note: This is an Alternate Cover Edition for ASIN: B00IFV9AXY.</i><br/><br/>It's said that women and men are from two different planets when it comes to communication, but how can they overcome the obstacles of prehistoric times when one of them simply doesn't have the ability to comprehend language?<br/><br/>Ehd's a caveman living on his own in a harsh wilderness. He's strong and int</span>
  <span id="freeText15785601057483061866" style="display:none"><i>Librarian's note: This is an Alternate Cover Edition for ASIN: B00IFV9AXY.</i><br /><br />It's said that women and men are from two different planets when it comes to communication, but how can they overcome the obstacles of prehistoric times when one of them simply doesn't have the ability to comprehend language?<br /><br />Ehd's a caveman living on his own in a harsh wilderness. He's strong and intelligent, but completely alone. When he finds a beautiful young woman in his pit trap, it's obvious to him that she is meant to be his mate. He doesn't know where she came from, she's wearing some pretty odd clothing, and she makes a lot of noises with her mouth that give him a headache. Still, he's determined to fulfill his purpose in life - provide for her, protect her, and put a baby in her.<br /><br />Elizabeth doesn't know where she is or exactly how she got there. She's confused and distressed by her predicament, and there's a caveman hauling her back to his cavehome. She's not at all interested in Ehd's primitive advances, and she just can't seem to get him to listen. No matter what she tries, getting her point across to this primitive but beautiful man is a constant - and often hilarious - struggle.<br /><br />With only each other for company, they must rely on one another to fight the dangers of the wild and prepare for the winter months. As they struggle to coexist, theirs becomes a love story that transcends language and time.</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Definitely read the author's notes (you can get that part in the Kindle preview without purchasing). If you are definitely looking for historical accu<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Definitely read the author's notes (you can get that part in the Kindle preview without purchasing). If you are definitely looking for historical accuracy, this isn't your book. It's meant to be fun, not accurate. Ehd isn't Neanderthal - he's Homo savage, my own creation for the sake of creating the atmosphere I wanted. :) <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

But then she had two more children?? In the end she took that injection and became infertile, which makes sense. It was before that I am wondering about. Edh noticed it up by her shoulder. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></a>

<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/27688701-sarah"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1462868448i/27688701.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/27688701-sarah">Sarah</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    It's never explained but I'm guessing that when her Dad brought Lah back he gave her two kinds of birth control, one that was temporary and would wear<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    It's never explained but I'm guessing that when her Dad brought Lah back he gave her two kinds of birth control, one that was temporary and would wear off after a few years and one that was permanent and would make her barren. She used the first because she had two very young children and knew they couldn't handle a third right then but didn't yet want to give up ever having another child. She finally used the second permanent birth control after her fourth child who, unlike her other children, could not understand her and must have gotten his brain development from his father's DNA instead of hers. <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer843685793" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9344176925378419755">ok I've been reading the reviews for this and am getting a little disturbed. reviewers are going on and on about how excited they are to read a romance that features a Neanderthal. come on, ladies. Neanderthals aren't even our own species! well I suppose they are a subspecies of the homo sapien. but still. I bet there's not a single Neanderthal in Transcendence.<br/><br/>now here is an example of a Neanderthal:<br/><br/><a href='http://s181.photobucket.com/user/markmonday/media/neanlooking_zps92b89351.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>do you seriously want that Neanderthal all over you? really?<br/><br/><a href='http://s181.photobucket.com/user/markmonday/media/image_zps1d40b6d0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>or how about this fellow...<br/><br/><a href='http://s181.photobucket.com/user/markmonday/media/neanderthal_zps28520e0f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
</a></span>

</a><br><br>or how about this fellow...<br><br><a href="http://s181.photobucket.com/user/markmonday/media/neanderthal_zps28520e0f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391468514i/8394206._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo neanderthal_zps28520e0f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>sisters, what you are looking for is a <b>CRO-MAGNON</b> man.<br><br>here's a typical Cro-Magnon hunk:<br><br><a href="http://s181.photobucket.com/user/markmonday/media/cro-magnon-stone-age-man_zpsb3c814e5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391468514i/8394207._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo cro-magnon-stone-age-man_zpsb3c814e5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>hubba hubba! you know you want to get with that.<br><br>even the professor below recognizes the charisma and sex appeal of the Cro-Magnon stud:<br><br><a href="http://s181.photobucket.com/user/markmonday/media/untitled_zpsf1c848d8.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391468514i/8394208._SX540_.png" alt=" photo untitled_zpsf1c848d8.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>so get it straight, please. NO to Neanderthals! YES to Cro-Magnons. there is a reason why Cro-Magnons survived and Neanderthals went the way of the dinosaur: it's 'cause those Cro-Magnons were so darned cute, obviously.<br><br>❤<br><br><i>I finally got around to reading this! below is a review, with spoilers:</i><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[my experience with romance novels is fairly minimal (although I do have a bit of experience - it is a genre I find fascinating), so I wasn't sure what to make of this one when I was reading it. it just felt so unusual to me, and refreshing. can something be refreshing if you haven't been burnt out on other things like it? I dunno. but this was a charming read and had me smiling throughout.<br><br>I thought when I started trying out romance novels a bit ago that I would be attracted to the darker, more fucked up romances, particularly since my favorite so far is the very morbid <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/425516.The_Silver_Devil" title="The Silver Devil by Teresa Denys" rel="nofollow noopener">The Silver Devil</a>. but I loved the lightness and the warmth in this one. it could also be that I've been in a cheerful mood these days and the novel didn't take me away from that.<br><br>I had some issues with Ehd's internal voice - mainly the language he used and the way he described things. didn't really seem to fit how a prehistoric type would think. but that was easy to let go of and after a while it didn't bother me at all. the repetitiousness of some of Ehd's commentary annoyed me in the beginning as well - until it didn't. it began to feel like the way a person like Ehd would actually think. it became sorta cute too, with his constant focus on Beth's strangeness and his frequent desire to "put a baby in her".<br><br>so Ehd was adorable and so was "Beh" - I actually liked her character just as much. her excitement at being able to make useful things was a lot of fun.<br><br>about halfway through I began to wonder if there would actually be a sex scene and then BOOM here comes the very graphic sex and there sure was a lot of it. but it is hard for me to consider this an erotic novel, no matter how explicitly the sex was described. I wasn't turned on... I was charmed! the sex scenes were sweet and even heartwarming, which kept me cheerful because these are two virginal kids just discovering sex. I wish sex could be as positive an experience for all virgins.<br><br>I loved the whole set-up of the story. it was interesting reading something that was about living in a prehistoric world on a day-to-day basis, the minutiae in the descriptions. how to stay safe, how to stay warm, how to prepare for winter, etc. I suppose some could find the repetitiveness of the storyline to be tedious but I found it to be absorbing. there is also something fascinating to me about a story that is solely concerned with a man and a woman loving each other in this time period - and with no interest in telling any other story but that one basic story. being set in a prehistoric time made the love story intriguingly stark.<br><br>I loved where the novel went, that sure was unexpected. the story follows them until they die in each other's arms at a nicely old age. it was so tender, so loving. for a long time I was wondering where the title would come in, and hey there it is at the end, and it made perfect sense. this is mainly a 3 star book for me (and I like my 3 star books, it's not a bad rating)... but I was quite moved by its gentle ending.<br><br>liked the minor science fiction rationale in the epilogue. clever!<br><br>overall the book was original and highly enjoyable. I'd recommend it to Romance readers but I don't really know what "Romance readers" are generally into. I hope they like this sort of romance.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9344176925378419755" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_833307104" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/833307104" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/833307104?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833307104" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15715704365683061672"><b>5 I Luffed this book Stars! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/d12550b4-58e1-45d4-ac40-99ed1365b9ed_zps93318d62.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393709828i/8755180.jpg' alt=' photo d12550b4-58e1-45d4-ac40-99ed1365b9ed_zps93318d62.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Transcendence was unlike any book I have ever read. To be honest, after reading the blurb I wasn’t too sure if it sounded like something I would like. After hearing a few friends rave about it, I decided to give it a go. I’m so happy I did. A beautiful, moving, and original story told in the pov of Edh, our caveman.<br/><br/>Edh has been living alone for a long time. After his tribe was destroyed many seasons ago, he was the only survivor. Going at it alone isn’t easy. He l</span>
  <span id="freeText15715704365683061672" style="display:none"><b>5 I Luffed this book Stars! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/d12550b4-58e1-45d4-ac40-99ed1365b9ed_zps93318d62.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393709828i/8755180.jpg" alt=" photo d12550b4-58e1-45d4-ac40-99ed1365b9ed_zps93318d62.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Transcendence was unlike any book I have ever read. To be honest, after reading the blurb I wasn’t too sure if it sounded like something I would like. After hearing a few friends rave about it, I decided to give it a go. I’m so happy I did. A beautiful, moving, and original story told in the pov of Edh, our caveman.<br><br>Edh has been living alone for a long time. After his tribe was destroyed many seasons ago, he was the only survivor. Going at it alone isn’t easy. He longs for companionship. One day out of no where, Edh finds a girl in a trap he set. She is dressed in clothing he’s never seen and she’s making strange noises, but it’s okay. He’s just happy not to be alone anymore. The girl gets out that her name is Beh. Edh decides Beh will be his mate. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/d2927762-2ecd-4f6b-a621-d3d25f758739_zpsb2824020.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393709828i/8755181.jpg" alt=" photo d2927762-2ecd-4f6b-a621-d3d25f758739_zpsb2824020.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Beh doesn’t seem like any of the women of his tribe, and he doesn’t understand. He wants to get her to like him, to show her that she will be safe and provided for with him, but he feels like he is failing. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I had thought getting her to like me would be fairly simple, but now that I have shown her everything I have, she seems bored, and I do not feel like a very good mate.”</blockquote>
</i><br>It takes some time, but slowly Beh starts to warm up to him. After spending more time with her, he realizes how happy he is not to be alone anymore. He isn’t so focused on ‘mating’. He doesn’t care that she’s different, or that she doesn’t seem to be able to communicate with him just yet. He only wants her to be there with him. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“She may be strange; she may not know how to make baskets, and she may be very noisy, but she is my mate, and I’m thrilled she is here.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/103fa081-6c99-4201-a260-5b10d7849c68_zpsfb3834a4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393709828i/8755182.jpg" alt=" photo 103fa081-6c99-4201-a260-5b10d7849c68_zpsfb3834a4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>She’s my mate, she’s unusual, and she’s mine.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>It takes Beh some time to come around. I’m sure she is not used to Edh’s ways, and she doesn’t know whats going on at first. Once she gets to see the real Edh, and see what kind of heart he has, she can’t help but start to fall for him. Edh was the sweetest, most kind and caring man. I had the biggest smile on my face for a majority of the book. Every time I heard him ask for a ‘khzz’ or tell Beh he ‘luffed’ her, I melted.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/5a1becbd-187b-4403-8d80-5651592d9036_zpse12c649e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393709828i/8755183.jpg" alt=" photo 5a1becbd-187b-4403-8d80-5651592d9036_zpse12c649e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The chemistry between these two was smoking hot! But it wasn’t just sexual. This book was filled with so many beautiful and tender moments between these two. Some brought me to tears, one straight up had me crying<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <b>I wonder what I will do if she doesn't wake up, and I don't have an answer. As I lie back down next to her and pull her into my arms, my stomach growls, and suddenly I know exactly what I will do. If she doesn't wake up, then I will just lie with her until I don't wake up either. </b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Even though there is no real dialogue between these two, you can feel the love they share. It is beautiful and moving to see how love can grow between to people so different, different times, different cultures, different languages. It just proves that love is limitless. Love grows through actions, not just words. <br><br>This book was so different and unique. I never thought this concept would appeal to me, but I can honestly say that I loved every bit of this book. Just a heads up, this book has little to no dialogue. It is told from Edh’s pov, so you mainly get his thoughts. Being inside his head was a joy. <br><br>Transcendence was a truly beautiful romance and one that stayed on my mind for days after read. I can already tell this is going to be on my favorites list for 2014! If you’re looking for a fresh and unique romance, pick this one up! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/27e52d73-2084-4852-98cc-a67e65118fdc_zps2b3ae5c5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393709828i/8755184.jpg" alt=" photo 27e52d73-2084-4852-98cc-a67e65118fdc_zps2b3ae5c5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15715704365683061672" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer856493543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11815698642190799945"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462526935i/19008370.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461582073ra/18883320.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462382146ra/18990869.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462459285ra/19000195.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>★★★★★! Transcendence (stand-alone). Ehd & Beh’s epic love story set in pre-historic times!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Love,” she whispers.<br/>“Luffs!” I respond, and her smile brightens even more.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/>Be-still-my-beating-heart! <b>Transcendence</b> (stand-alone) is an <b>epic love saga in pre-historic times!</b><br/><br/>Story opens up to <b>caveman Ehd,</b> separated from his tribe, finding a peculiar woman in his trap, <b>Elizabeth, Beh.</b> His instinct is to protect her, his baser needs to put a baby in her, but his heart shows him how to </span>
  <span id="freeText11815698642190799945" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462526935i/19008370.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461582073ra/18883320.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462382146ra/18990869.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462459285ra/19000195.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>★★★★★! Transcendence (stand-alone). Ehd &amp; Beh’s epic love story set in pre-historic times!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Love,” she whispers.<br>“Luffs!” I respond, and her smile brightens even more.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Be-still-my-beating-heart! <b>Transcendence</b> (stand-alone) is an <b>epic love saga in pre-historic times!</b><br><br>Story opens up to <b>caveman Ehd,</b> separated from his tribe, finding a peculiar woman in his trap, <b>Elizabeth, Beh.</b> His instinct is to protect her, his baser needs to put a baby in her, but his heart shows him how to love her and be a family.<br><br>We get to <b>follow Ehd and Beh</b> through their out-of-times meeting, awkward courtship, brewing love and on through life’s ups and downs. Faced with the dangers of their era they <b>fight</b> to survive, <b>learn</b> to persevere and <b>strive</b> to progress set against the backdrop of Ehd’s love for Beh.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462526935ra/19008371.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Four words to describe <b>Ehd: Protective, charming, noble and sweet</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462526935ra/19008372.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Four words to describe <b>Elizabeth, Beh: Brave, moody, nurturing and complacent</b>.<br><br><b>Transcendence,</b> told from Ehd’s POV, depicts a <b>love so great it transcends time!</b> Their story ends full circle, bringing tears to my eyes.<br><br>Spectacular! Unforgettable! Epic! Thought-provoking!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Beh loves Ehd.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 4 stars<br>Sexual tension rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br>Plot rating: 4.5 stars<br>Dialogue rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 5 stars<br>**********************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this book: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br>Thank you to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1080296685?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Liz</a> for Buddy-reading!<br><br><b>
  <i>Signed paperback provided to me by author Shay Savage in exchange for an honest review, but I purchased my own Kindle copy.</i>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1301569739?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="V. A Court of Wings and Ruin is NEW ADULT/EROTICA but Goodreads editors won&#39;t tell you to include it in the choice awards" class="user" itemprop="url" name="V.         rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of my mate repeated to the infinite</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31006810-v-a-court-of-wings-and-ruin-is-new-adult-erotica-but-goodreads-editors?shelf=strongfemales">strongfemales</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31006810-v-a-court-of-wings-and-ruin-is-new-adult-erotica-but-goodreads-editors?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31006810-v-a-court-of-wings-and-ruin-is-new-adult-erotica-but-goodreads-editors?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31006810-v-a-court-of-wings-and-ruin-is-new-adult-erotica-but-goodreads-editors?shelf=diversity">diversity</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31006810-v-a-court-of-wings-and-ruin-is-new-adult-erotica-but-goodreads-editors?shelf=safe-read">safe-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31006810-v-a-court-of-wings-and-ruin-is-new-adult-erotica-but-goodreads-editors?shelf=no-slut-shaming">no-slut-shaming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31006810-v-a-court-of-wings-and-ruin-is-new-adult-erotica-but-goodreads-editors?shelf=no-insta-love">no-insta-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1301569739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14456143533536185473"><b>Update 09-01-2017 A famous author whose name I won't mention because her fans are scary ;) borrowed heavily from this SELF-PUBLISHED book. Anyone who loves the words "my mate" repeated endlessly should read this book</b><br/><br/><b>Update October 11th. I wish more people knew about this book because I found no cheating and no slut shaming. Books that don't promote violence on women like Transcendence and are still steamy and compelling deserve more love.</b><br/>Jared Padalecki as shaved Ehd<br/><br/>ORIGINAL REVIEW<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454203573i/17930794._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Before I write</span>
  <span id="freeText14456143533536185473" style="display:none"><b>Update 09-01-2017 A famous author whose name I won't mention because her fans are scary ;) borrowed heavily from this SELF-PUBLISHED book. Anyone who loves the words "my mate" repeated endlessly should read this book</b><br><br><b>Update October 11th. I wish more people knew about this book because I found no cheating and no slut shaming. Books that don't promote violence on women like Transcendence and are still steamy and compelling deserve more love.</b><br>Jared Padalecki as shaved Ehd<br><br>ORIGINAL REVIEW<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454203573i/17930794._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Before I write my review of Surviving Raine it's fair that I review one of my 2015 favorites. I re-read Trascendence because I wanted to have a feel of the author's style before I dived into Survaiving Raine. My conclusion? I'm a huge fan Of Mrs. Savage. <i> (Update Oct 10th, Not anymore after I tried her scifi books and read the spoilers for Surviving Raine sequels , but this book is fantastic)</i><br><br>We meet Ehd, a caveman who lives in the Ice-Age. He's also the loneliest man on the planet. He lost his tribe to a fire, all his family. He has struggled to survive these rough times. He doesn't have much of a life. He's SURVIVING. He hadn't seen another human being for a long time and Ehd's starting to think that he'll be alone forever.<br><br>A modern-day girl named Elizabeth appears magically. It's never clear how that happens but you can imagine the 20000 years age of cultural differences that separte these soon-to-be-couple. Ehd is determined to mate with her and surely you understand all the sexy implications of that decision.<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434564630i/15238309.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Or should I say instict? Because Ehd is a very primitive man whose actions are driven by instict and eventually by LOVE.<br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454202998ra/17930757.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454203227i/17930769.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He'll provide for her, he'll protect her from harm and he'll put a baby on her. A baby! That's cute and sexy at the same time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454203509i/17930792.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>What I love about this book is that we are all the time on Ehd's mind and his train of thought is amazing. He's naive, but strong, and he falls in love hard for his mate. He's extremely repetitive. <i>My mate, I have to provide for my mate, she is my mate my mate is weird, I want my mate with me, I have to protect my mate</i> . It's really primitive, cute and charming at the same time.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1476047581i/20796125._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how this couple falls for each other slowly, how they solve their cultural differences and how, what started as a very instictive desire (I have to put a baby on her) ended up in a love that TRASCENDS THE TIME. Love trascends everything. I think just the title was so full of promise and the book delivered.<br><br>The steamy scenes are full of that longing, cuteness and awkwardness of two virgin people who are learning to love. That's the reason I read New Adult and Classic romance. This kind of storyline is always so romantic because it's like inexperience is another burden for a couple to overcome and when they do it correctly is always so romantic. Beh and Ehd journey to survive the harsh times they live in and at the same time discover love is one of the best I've read. It's beautiful.<br><br>My only minor complain about the book is that perhaps just a little less sex would have worked better for me, and a I wish there had beem a little bit of Beh's perspective. That would have made a huge difference in an already-awesome-book, but at the end I don't care. I just started to try to put bookmarks on my favorite lines and without meaning it, I ended up re-reading the whole book. FOR THE THIRD TIME. I have a lot of homework and tons of books to read, but couldn't stop. That's how much I love this book and why is one of 2015 favorites.<br><br>I have to appreciate how cute this story was and I can't describe it in words properly. I just love how original this is. No billionaires, no tattoed boys, no clones of Anastasia steele or aby abernathy OR bELLA Swan. The two characters feel real and refreshing. You have to suspend disbelief a lot, because some times Ehd is just too perfect and the traveling from one age to the other is not explained, but who cares? The book is an incredibly, fast-paced journey.<br><br>If you haven't read this book, what are you waiting for? Even if you don't like fantasy book and prefer a contemporary setting perhaps you will enjoy Shay Savage's contemporary romances. I know I did.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/854997788" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/854997788?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer854997788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8416383949782043438"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/transcendence_zpsc50fea67.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395700072i/9032263.jpg' alt=' photo transcendence_zpsc50fea67.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>When I started reading Transcendence by Shay Savage, I thought I knew what to expect. I read the synopsis and knew the basics of the book. But…I was wrong. I was not prepared at all for this book. How it would make me both laugh and cry. At the intensity of the feelings it would evoke.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/index_zps632d916d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395700072i/9032264.jpg' alt=' photo index_zps632d916d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>Ehd is a caveman, and he is alone and so very lonely. He has been alone for a very long time. This last winter has been hard, but he wonders if maybe it was so hard because he is losing the will to survive</span>
  <span id="freeText8416383949782043438" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/transcendence_zpsc50fea67.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395700072i/9032263.jpg" alt=" photo transcendence_zpsc50fea67.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When I started reading Transcendence by Shay Savage, I thought I knew what to expect. I read the synopsis and knew the basics of the book. But…I was wrong. I was not prepared at all for this book. How it would make me both laugh and cry. At the intensity of the feelings it would evoke.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/index_zps632d916d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395700072i/9032264.jpg" alt=" photo index_zps632d916d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Ehd is a caveman, and he is alone and so very lonely. He has been alone for a very long time. This last winter has been hard, but he wonders if maybe it was so hard because he is losing the will to survive. But that all changes as one day he finds a beautiful woman in his pit trap. This woman looks nothing like any female he has ever seen. The coverings on her body and on her feet are completely unfamiliar. And the sounds coming out of her mouth are giving him a headache. But, she is beautiful, and she is his.<br><br><i>
  <b>“I will provide for her. I will protect her. I will give her anything she wants.”</b>
</i><br><br>Elizabeth finds herself trapped in a deep pit. And her rescuer is a beautiful man wearing nothing but some pieces of animal hide. He hauls her out of the pit and to his cave. He doesn’t seem to understand anything she says. But, very quickly he does learn the meaning of the word “no!” She very quickly realizes, though, that she must depend on this man for survival, to protect her in this unknown wilderness. Their tenuous relationship does turn to a somewhat comfortable partnership, as long as Ehd respects Beh’s use of the word “no.” And soon their relationship begins to slowly grow into love.<br><br><i>
  <b>“My mate, My Beh”</b>
</i><br><br>Ehd and Beh are faced with the task of understanding each other without being able to verbally communicate. Men seem to have a hard enough time understanding the complexities of the female mind. So I can understand Ehd’s frustration with trying to figure out Beh. The book is told from his point of view and it is hilarious at times watching him struggle.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I don’t understand, but when it comes to my mate, I rarely do.”</i>
</b><br><br>But, the power of love overcomes all obstacles. With all the differences Beh and Ehd are faced with, they learn to depend on one another, they respect one another, and they support one another. So, buckle your seat belt. Don’t plan on getting much accomplished, get yourself a comfortable reading spot, and read this book. I will not be forgetting Beh and Ehd anytime soon. I hope you feel the same way, too. Thank you, Shay Savage, for a beautiful book.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/skeleton_zps4732aa2e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395700072i/9032265.jpg" alt=" photo skeleton_zps4732aa2e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Note: This book does contain adult content so is for the appropriate reader only.<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8416383949782043438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=top-reads-of-all-time">top-reads-of-all-time</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer843205494" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14942367227310299669">If I could give this more than 5 stars I would.<br/><br/>This was such a beautiful story. Ehd was such a "pure" character in the sense that he lived honestly and simply, according to his instincts and emotions. He never had ulterior motives. He just wanted Beh to be his mate and to provide for her and make a family with her.<br/><br/>Just the fact that Shay Savage was able to conceive and write this amazing story - a story in which there are only really two characters and virtually NO dialogue - is a testament to w</span>
  <span id="freeText14942367227310299669" style="display:none">If I could give this more than 5 stars I would.<br /><br />This was such a beautiful story. Ehd was such a "pure" character in the sense that he lived honestly and simply, according to his instincts and emotions. He never had ulterior motives. He just wanted Beh to be his mate and to provide for her and make a family with her.<br /><br />Just the fact that Shay Savage was able to conceive and write this amazing story - a story in which there are only really two characters and virtually NO dialogue - is a testament to what a great author she is. The fact that she writes the story through Ehd's eyes and stays true to the premise that Ehd cannot understand ANYTHING Beh is saying is true talent.<br /><br />I loved how she was able to make us really feel how frustrated Ehd would become at not understanding what Beh wanted or why she was mad at him. Also, the way in which Savage was able to convey what Beh was saying to the reader without actually using words, merely Ehd's observations and inferences - and not actual dialogue - really made the story and the setting authentic.<br /><br />And the ending, oh the ending. So beautiful. <br /><br />This book is definitely on my all time favorite list. I think I'm gonna go read it again...</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833106089" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2949600418718766691">★★★★★ <b>4.5 stars!</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392226056i/8521543.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What an amazing story! I absolutely LOVED everything about it. Once again, Shay Savage has delivered an outstanding male point of view that managed to keep me hooked from the moment I started reading it. And most of all, she has created another unique, swoon worthy hero that managed to sweep me off my feet with just a few of his many achingly sweet and adoringly funny gestures.<br/>In essence, Transcendence is a <b>love story</b> but it is also a story about survival, communication, hope an</span>
  <span id="freeText2949600418718766691" style="display:none">★★★★★ <b>4.5 stars!</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392226056i/8521543.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What an amazing story! I absolutely LOVED everything about it. Once again, Shay Savage has delivered an outstanding male point of view that managed to keep me hooked from the moment I started reading it. And most of all, she has created another unique, swoon worthy hero that managed to sweep me off my feet with just a few of his many achingly sweet and adoringly funny gestures.<br>In essence, Transcendence is a <b>love story</b> but it is also a story about survival, communication, hope and the courage to fight for what you want and about finding love in the most unexpected places.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390917872i/8297991.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caveman <b>Ehd</b> has been on his own for quite some time. Ever since his family and the rest of his clan died, he's been living in solitude while trying to survive the ever-changing seasons in the barren land where he lives. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I have no idea how long it has been since I felt the comfort of another person's presence, only that many cold seasons have passed since then."</i>
</blockquote><br>Then, on one of his hunts, he suddenly stumbles upon a young, beautiful girl who has fallen into his pit trap. Ehd is immediately taken away with her beauty and he couldn't be happier with his discovery since it seems he's finally found his long awaited mate.<br><br>Elizabeth ("Beh"), on the other hand, has no idea where is she or how she's gotten there. She went from the twenty first century she grew up in to suddenly landing in this prehistoric age populated by cavemen who have no knowledge of the English language. It's extremely hard for her to adjust to her new conditions and at first she tries to keep her distance from Ehd as much as possible, even though he's the only other person around who's able to help her survive.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390948387i/8303831.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As the story progresses both Ehd and Beh have many struggles to overcome; the most important one being their lack of communication. Ehd doesn't speak English so every single one of their "conversations" has to go through a bit of sign language and facial expressions. Then, there's also the fact that Ehd first and only thought is that Beh is his new mate and he wants to put a baby inside her so they can form a family. Of course, that's not how it works in our century and when Beh keeps turning him down he has to find new ways to make her like and care for him. Along the way, his feelings for her grow stronger and he begins to realize all he really wants is for her to just be there with him, not just as his mate but as his partner as well.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"There is nothing more important than Beh, and if making her happy means my own sorrow, I will have to accept that."</i>
</blockquote><br>Even though there is practically no dialogue and the entire story is told from Ehd's POV, Beh and Ehd still managed to communicate their love for each other beautifully and that is exactly what made their love so <b>epic</b>. Ehd never failed to show her with his actions that he was willing to do anything to protect her and make her happy and Beh on the other hand, tried to show him with the few words she was able to teach him how much he meant to her as well. They were both such strong characters and I can't even begin to imagine what life must have been like for Beh to adjust to her new life conditions. Together though, they tried to be there for each other whenever the other one was going through a difficult time and they managed to make to most of the life conditions they were given. <br><br>All in all, this unique, captivating, heartfelt and at times hilarious love story is an <b>absolute must read</b>. And let's face it, you do not want to miss meeting caveman Ehd, I assure you! ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392226056i/8521544.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Release date:</b> February 14, 2014.<br><br><b>
  <i>**ARC kindly provided by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5072145.L_J__Anderson" title="L.J. Anderson" rel="nofollow noopener">L.J. Anderson</a> on behalf of the author in exchange for an honest review**</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_1417354532" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1417354532" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1417354532?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1417354532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8436697898470919930"><b>5 Stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445349857i/16636770.jpg' width='400' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>“Transcendence”</i> by Shay Savage was unlike anything I have read. It was such a unique, beautiful, unforgettable, tough-provoking story. This book moved me to my core and it will stay with me for a long time. I love this author’s writing style. I really do. But I have to admit I was reluctant to start this book simply because it’s labeled as a historical romance. I have read a few historical romances, but honestly it’s not one of my favorite genre. So if you are like me and you don’t have</span>
  <span id="freeText8436697898470919930" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445349857i/16636770.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Transcendence”</i> by Shay Savage was unlike anything I have read. It was such a unique, beautiful, unforgettable, tough-provoking story. This book moved me to my core and it will stay with me for a long time. I love this author’s writing style. I really do. But I have to admit I was reluctant to start this book simply because it’s labeled as a historical romance. I have read a few historical romances, but honestly it’s not one of my favorite genre. So if you are like me and you don’t have necessarily a thing for this genre, think again and pick this book up. You won’t regret it!<br><br>This book left me speechless. The story, the characters, the writing were done to perfection IMO. The story is a story about love. That kind of love that is pure, simple, beautiful. <i>“Transcendence”</i> is the story of Ehd, a caveman in prehistoric times. He lives alone since all the men and women in his tribe died. He feels alone and he longs for companionship. One day he finds a strange woman in one of his pit traps. The woman wears strange clothes and makes weird noises, but Ehd is sure that she’s the most beautiful woman he’d ever seen. He decides to keep this strange woman, to provide for her, to protect her and to put a baby in her belly, so he decides to make her his mate. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I will provide for her. I will protect her. I will give her anything she wants.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Elizabeth (Beh) doesn’t know where she is or how she got there. She is scared, a little injured and frustrated because she can’t communicate with this strange, yet good looking man. She is terrified when this man takes her to his cave. But he doesn’t want to hurt her. If at the beginning she is frightened by Ehd, as time passes she starts to warm up to him. Ehd wants to make Beh his mate, but first he must make her like him. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I want her; I know I do. It is far beyond not wanting to be alone anymore. I want her – only her. I will do anything to make Beh mine.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ehd and Beh get to know each other and they start to communicate in their own way. It’s hard for both of them, but they learn how to be patient with the other, they learn things from each other and they eventually become mates starting a new family. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“My Beh, my mate.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Written entirely from Ehd’s POV, <i>“Transcending”</i> was very different from what I usually read. First because the story is written from a caveman’s perspective and secondly because there’s no real dialogue. I can’t remember the last book I have read without any real dialogue, so obviously I was a little scared about this aspect of the story. At least in the beginning. I’m glad to say the story was pure and simple perfection even without any real dialogue. Needless to say I couldn’t put it down. The story doesn’t have any action and overall you can say is very slow, but I liked it very much.<br><br>Ehd was a character that won me over from the beginning. He’s innocent and naïve, maybe a little frustrating at times, but he was so adorable and kind. His need to protect and provide for Beh was so sweet. His need to comfort her at times and the way he cared for her and later loved her melt me in a puddle of goo. His tenderness was simply wonderful. It goes without saying that I liked this strange caveman more than other possessive/caveman heroes I read about. Being in Ehd’s head was a strange, yet very unique experience. Every time, this author knows how to write effortlessly a male POV and this time she did it again. Our caveman’s POV felt so honest and genuine and I truly enjoyed it. He made me smile and swoon so many times. However, I would have liked at least one chapter from Beh’s poin-of-view. I wanted to know what she thinks and what she feels for Ehd.<br><br>I don’t know if I can say that was a chemistry between these two characters. Since there’s no real dialogue it's hard to say. But there’s was a connection there. They not only learned how to survive together, they also learned how to understand, accept and love each other.<br> <br>Overall, a wonderful, touching read that I highly recommend!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”My life with Beh was beautiful, trascending everything that set us apart from each other..."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="8436697898470919930" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/904729153?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nataliya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nataliya" href="/user/show/3672777-nataliya">Nataliya</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3672777-nataliya?shelf=2014-reads">2014-reads</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer904729153" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13813782989244937221">Sometimes I read books just for the sheer hilarity. Or awesome riveting dialogue. Like the one heavily featured in this book: <blockquote>
  <i>"Ehd.... Beh..... Ehd..... Beh..... Ehd...... Beh...."</i>
</blockquote> Irresistible, right? Right? Right? Right?... Bueller? Bueller?... Bueller?...<br/><br/>A young woman from our present is somehow transported into the prehistoric times and comes across an idealized version of a prehistoric man who is dead-set on sexxxing her up, after a thoughtful courtship, of course. Let me note that she </span>
  <span id="freeText13813782989244937221" style="display:none">Sometimes I read books just for the sheer hilarity. Or awesome riveting dialogue. Like the one heavily featured in this book: <blockquote>
  <i>"Ehd.... Beh..... Ehd..... Beh..... Ehd...... Beh...."</i>
</blockquote> Irresistible, right? Right? Right? Right?... Bueller? Bueller?... Bueller?...<br><br>A young woman from our present is somehow transported into the prehistoric times and comes across an idealized version of a prehistoric man who is dead-set on sexxxing her up, after a thoughtful courtship, of course. Let me note that she seems more attracted to him after she forces him to brush his prehistoric messy hair and take a prehistoric bath. <b>He, on the other hand, is fascinated by her lacy pink bra and panties, which - unless I'm completely misunderstanding something here - she has not changed for a few months </b>(the absence of lingerie stores in prehistoric times is a bummer). <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401046403i/9750632._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ehd, the prehistoric dude, is unable to comprehend speech or learn to speak (some Broca's area nonsense here), and therefore communicates in grunts (so basically like a stoned frat boy on a Thursday night, really). <br><br>Unable to comprehend the speech of his new lover, he dismisses it as silly noises - but does catch on quickly that certain 'noises' if he stupidly makes them guarantee him sexxxxy prehistoric times, and so those are the only words he bothers to learn. Otherwise he shortens the young woman's name to 'Beh' and thus the suspenseful dialogue ensues:<blockquote>
  <i>"Ehd.... Beh..... Ehd..... Beh..... Ehd...... Beh...."</i>
</blockquote>Wait. Wait. Wait. Waaaaaait.<blockquote>
  <i>Ehd.<br>Beh.</i>
</blockquote>A vapid heroine with a dishrag personality who is somehow the center of the hero's world.<br>An uber-possessive overly-protective hero with messy copper-colored hair and a flair for codependent relationships.<br><br>I've read it before, somewhere. I swear, this is so familiar...<blockquote>
  <i>Ehd?<br>Beh?</i>
</blockquote> Oh crap.<blockquote>
  <b>Edward?<br>Bella?</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401046403i/9750633._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>This was 'Twilight' fanfic? Ahhhhhhhh.......<br><br><br>Well, that explains a lot.</b><br><br>The awkwardness. The lack of communication. The angst. The creepy overprotectiveness. The codependency. The lack of plot.<br><br><b>It still does not explain the supposed attractiveness of unwashed sex in a cave with a guy who dismisses any attempts at verbal communications as meaningless noise. </b><br><br>Unless, of course, this 'noise' results in sex.<br>And babies.<br><br>Blergh.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13813782989244937221" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/840195838?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer840195838" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10478381780624390023"><b>4 I just fell for a caveman stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392519054i/8572622._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>
  <b>I will provide for her. I will give her anything she wants.</b>

It was unlike anything I have ever read and I doubt I'd rea</span>
  <span id="freeText10478381780624390023" style="display:none"><b>4 I just fell for a caveman stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392519054i/8572622._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>I will provide for her. I will give her anything she wants.</b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Have you ever wondered if it is possible to read a book that only has about 4 words of dialogue yet still love it?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388371055ra/7812685.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Have you also ever wondered of what would happen if a prehistoric book mated with a Nicholas Sparks book? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392606959ra/8583637.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If I was a fan of Shay Savage before reading this, I am now full on<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392606959ra/8583638.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This was an amazing, beautiful, one of a kind love story. It was unlike anything I have ever read and I doubt I'd read again. It was unique. It was unforgettable.<br><br>I struggled with my rating at first since it did take me a bit to get into the story. I did skim through some parts and found it to be slow in others. But considering it's been 2 days since I've finished and I still can't stop thinking about it? It deserves nothing less of the 4 glorious stars. <br><br>If you read the blurb and are expecting a domineering "caveman" caveman type alpha (You know the type. The "me man you woman we bang" type of caveman"), well you'll be sadly disappointed. Ehd was nothing like that.<br><br>He was vulnerable, sweet, constantly doubting himself with Beh, and at the same time so incredibly endearing that you can't help but completely fall for him. His inner thoughts never failed to put a smile on my face.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">What if I don't fit inside her?<br>After all this time of waiting for her to want me, what will I do if I am unable to mate with Beh?<br>I take a calming breath and assure myself I will fit inside of her. Women are supposed to stretch there so babies can be put inside and come back out when they're ready. If something the size of a baby can come out, surely my penis can go in.<br>It's big, but it't not that big!</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The story is told entirely in Ehd's POV. The fact that Shay Savage was able to write an entire book from a caveman's POV that has about 3 words in his whole vocabulary just shows her incredible talent as an author. It's no small feat let me tell you.<br><br>You don't get much more insight into Elizabeth that what Ehd is able to gather from his perspective. <br><br>It wasn't a quick paced book. There wasn't a lot of action, no dirty talk, or filthy dirty caveman loving. Don't get me wrong, it was still steamy, in a very sweet first time discovery way. Both Elizabeth, or Beh as he calls her, and Ehd are innocently naive. But that just added to the appeal for me.<br><br>It is told over the span of many years, and unfolds the story of love at it's most innocent and pure. It was beautiful, albeit not my usual type of book.<br><br>Then there was that ending. Oh my poor cold little heart, that ending!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387312687ra/7575047.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The only other time I cried like that was at the end of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The Notebook <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Good lord.<br><br>And just as you think it's over, Shay gives you a last chapter that just ties everything together.<br><br>Were there some discrepancies in the story? Sure. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[How can Elizabeth live her entire life in the tribe and even her children talk, but no one else in the tribe, not even Ehd pick up more words? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>But this is not really a book that you expect to be highly realistic, so I didn't harp on that.<br><br>So if you're looking for a different and unique book about a beautiful and innocent love and discovery, this is not to be missed. You will fall for Ehd just like I did. It's one of those books that will stick with you for a while.<br><br><i>***ARC given to Dirty Girl Romance blog in exchange for an honest review***</i><br><br>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14267242729106700239"><b>5+ Stars! A book that will be forever in my heart...<b></b><br/><br/>What can I say about this mind-reeling book?<br/><br/>I promised myself to only read the first chapter to get a feel for it...<br/>Yeah, right.<br/>Four and a half hours later, I had murdered this book, and myself in the meantime.<br/><br/>Never have I had emotions pulled from me like I had with Transcendence.<br/>I am still speechless.<br/><br/>It took me a little while to get used to the style of narration, but once I was in, I was IN. As in completely invested and wanting to learn more</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14267242729106700239" style="display:none"><b>5+ Stars! A book that will be forever in my heart...<b></b><br /><br />What can I say about this mind-reeling book?<br /><br />I promised myself to only read the first chapter to get a feel for it...<br />Yeah, right.<br />Four and a half hours later, I had murdered this book, and myself in the meantime.<br /><br />Never have I had emotions pulled from me like I had with Transcendence.<br />I am still speechless.<br /><br />It took me a little while to get used to the style of narration, but once I was in, I was IN. As in completely invested and wanting to learn more, turning pages as quickly as I could.<br />14% in, I had shed my first tears. Tears which would be the first of many. Don't misunderstand me. This is a LOVE STORY. About a committed couple who would do anything for one another. The love they share is special in a way that is a so beautiful, it will bring you to tears.<br /><br />Annnnd i'm crying again. (Damn you, Shay Savage!!!! You brilliant woman, you!)<br /><br />We get inside the mind of caveman, Ehd, who is a smart guy, although he has no way to express himself with words, he does a fine job with grunts, growls and actions. We begin the story at the very depths of his depression, for he is lonely. He has been alone for a long time. He only wants a mate. Companionship. Someone to share his life with.<br />Enter Elizabeth (AKA Beh). <br />I'm almost afraid to tell you more about this book. It is honestly not something I can tell you about. It is something you need to experience.<br />I normally need a lot of dialogue between characters to enjoy a book. This book doesn't have much dialogue and I'll be honest...it didn't need it. Not at all.<br />Unlike any book I've ever read.<br /><br />This book is now on my Top Five Favourite books... EVER!<br /><br />Get this book right now. You will laugh, cry and melt. You will fall in love with these characters and when they are in pain, you will feel it in your very soul.<br />A love story to top all love stories.</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer804097603409325444"><b> 4.5 "Ehd luffs Beh." stars</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/awe%201_zpsmuflqm5i.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

Loved being in his head. God he had me laughing so hard at some of his thoughts. I loved Beh, loved their relationship. The only reason this book wasn't a 5 star for me is because I wou</span>
  <span id="freeText804097603409325444" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 "Ehd luffs Beh." stars</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/awe%201_zpsmuflqm5i.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428961246ra/14508056.gif" alt=" photo awe 1_zpsmuflqm5i.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>We eat, I put my penis inside of her for a while, and then I fall back to sleep.</b><br><br><br>OMG this book blew me away. It has to be one of the most surprising and unique books I have ever read. This book is a funny, easy , feel good read. Ehd had some seriously sexy caveman charm. I loved him. Loved being in his head. God he had me laughing so hard at some of his thoughts. I loved Beh, loved their relationship. The only reason this book wasn't a 5 star for me is because I would have liked to hear what the others, Beh, Dad, and the kids were saying . I loved that the POV was all from Ehd's but if we could have heard just what the others said around him, especially Beh I feel like I could have got to know Beh better. Other than that this book was a awesomely sweet and I teared up at the end . I would totally recommend it!<br><br><b>Then she leans over and takes my penis in her mouth. "Hoh!" I sit up quickly, the shock of my mate's actions causing my body to react almost violently. Beh has my penis in her mouth. In her mouth! I can't put a baby in there!</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/black-and-white-couple-kiss-photography-pumarck-Favim.com-469805_zpsdduz9s4v.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428961246i/14508057._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo black-and-white-couple-kiss-photography-pumarck-Favim.com-469805_zpsdduz9s4v.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823172508" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2959835462922672212"><b>
  <i>”My life with Beh was beautiful, trascending everything that set us apart from each other..."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392521748i/8572900._SX540_.jpg' width='390' height='430' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>"Hoh!"</b> Shay Savage has written to <b>PERFECTION</b> the <b>FIRST ALPHA</b>. She takes us waaaay back in time to experience the love story of Ehd and Beh. <br/><br/>Ehd’s pov guides this whole story. He doesn’t possess the capacity for language. Needless to say, dialogue in this story is scarce.<br/> <br/>Ehd lost his family and has been surviving on his own. Up until one day he finds a beautiful girl making noises caught in his pit t</span>
  <span id="freeText2959835462922672212" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”My life with Beh was beautiful, trascending everything that set us apart from each other..."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392521748i/8572900._SX540_.jpg" width="390" height="430" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Hoh!"</b> Shay Savage has written to <b>PERFECTION</b> the <b>FIRST ALPHA</b>. She takes us waaaay back in time to experience the love story of Ehd and Beh. <br><br>Ehd’s pov guides this whole story. He doesn’t possess the capacity for language. Needless to say, dialogue in this story is scarce.<br> <br>Ehd lost his family and has been surviving on his own. Up until one day he finds a beautiful girl making noises caught in his pit trap. She is dressed oddly and uttering sounds that he doesn’t comprehend. <br><br>Ehd is hyped to make Beh his mate. He wants to provide for her, to protect her, and to impregnate her. Beh's responses confuses Ehd. It's pretty funny as a woman to read his prehistoric pov.<br><br><b>
  <i>”She is crying, but I don’t understand why. Was I already a bad mate for her? Was my cave really that inadequate”</i>
</b><br><br>It takes a while for Beh’s tears to stop, for her to respond favorably towards Ehd. I got the biggest kick at certain scenes as Beh assimilates to her new environment and mate.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Beh needs to make baskets, and I need to hunt. That’s how it works. Apparently, Beh doesn’t know this.”</i>
</b><br><br>Sometimes Ehd’s thoughts are on a loop of his priorities but for me it worked and I found him gentle, kind, sexy, protective and simply wonderful!<br><br><b>
  <i>”She may be strange; she may not know how to make baskets, and she may be very noisy, but she is my mate, and I’m thrilled she is here.”</i>
</b><br><br>Time passes and Ehd and Beh’s relationship grows deeper and deeper. Their sex scenes were on fire as these two explore one another and it surpasses all of Ehd’s expectations. <br> <br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>I can see how some may not get into this story. For me, this was extremely well done, unforgettable and I honestly cried that’s how moved I was by this story. <br><br>Through and through this was an unforgettable tale of luffs!<br><br><b>
  <i>"I tilt my head to the side, listening to the three short sounds she utters in a row."</i>
</b></span>
