<div id="review_3500287243" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3500287243" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3500287243?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3500287243" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3652760343438830980">The book that made me google <a href='https://youtu.be/wj0qx56cwOw' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Sex Life of Early Humans</a>. You’d be shocked by all the weird and revealing facts I found. Why, you learn something new every day.<br/><br/>A sexed up prehistoric romance told from the perspective of the male lead who doesn’t know how to speak because early humans don’t communicate through language and is horny all the time because he only has the brain capacity to mate, mate, and mate.<br/><br/>This book is undoubtedly odd. It’s unique in terms of the setting and time period, but eve</span>
  <span id="freeText3652760343438830980" style="display:none">The book that made me google <a href="https://youtu.be/wj0qx56cwOw" rel="nofollow noopener">The Sex Life of Early Humans</a>. You’d be shocked by all the weird and revealing facts I found. Why, you learn something new every day.<br /><br />A sexed up prehistoric romance told from the perspective of the male lead who doesn’t know how to speak because early humans don’t communicate through language and is horny all the time because he only has the brain capacity to mate, mate, and mate.<br /><br />This book is undoubtedly odd. It’s unique in terms of the setting and time period, but everything else is just meh. Sure, the romance is beautiful, but we have no plot whatsoever and no dialogue. I really can’t with the repetitive inner monologue of Ehd wanting to “provide” for Beh and “put a baby inside her.”<br /><br />Don’t get me worng, I loved Ehd’s pure and innocence, his protectiveness and primal caveman insticts. I loved all the daily mundane routine they do. I also appreciate that even though Ehd can’t understand anything Beh is saying, us readers can still draw together what’s going on through Ehd’s observations.<br /><br />Since the author claimed to have taken the liberty to make the book more <i>fun</i> and abandoned historical accuracy, I think making Beh teach Ehd how to speak would be awesome. There’s also a mention of some tribal conflict and if that had been explored more, I think it’d make for a great plot.<br /><br />If this . . . <i>situation</i> wasn’t romanticized, I think I’d find everything in this prehistoric world a turn off and that I wouldn’t survive a day in it—sexy caveman companion present or not.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_819033311" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/819033311" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/819033311?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer819033311" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3777936271812386355"><b>Shay Savage is master of writing untraditional, unconventional and unforgettable stories. And Transcedence definitely proves it. </b><br/><br/><i>What happens when lonely caveman Ehd finds strange girl near his cave? He takes her as his mate. But how will he make her like him when they cannot communicate? And so starts this original and exciting journey of two souls that might or might not be destined for each other...</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392405071i/8553020.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Transcendence is one of <b>the most unique</b> and interesting books I have ever read. I’m not sure if</span>
  <span id="freeText3777936271812386355" style="display:none"><b>Shay Savage is master of writing untraditional, unconventional and unforgettable stories. And Transcedence definitely proves it. </b><br><br><i>What happens when lonely caveman Ehd finds strange girl near his cave? He takes her as his mate. But how will he make her like him when they cannot communicate? And so starts this original and exciting journey of two souls that might or might not be destined for each other...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392405071i/8553020.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Transcendence is one of <b>the most unique</b> and interesting books I have ever read. I’m not sure if there is something similar out there. It was extremely fascinating experience to read about real caveman, his thinking, his way of living. And the most surprising thing of all? The fact that Ehd was sweet, caring and very sensitive person. <br><br>Yes, <b>Ehd</b> was manly man and made me laugh quite often with the way he was seeing things. I am used to jerk-like arrogant heroes in Mrs. Savage’s books and I love them. But Ehd was nothing like that. Yet, he really grew on me quickly and made an excellent narrator for this story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392405071i/8553021._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But most importantly, Transcendence is an <b>epic love story</b>. Sounds unbeliavable when it comes to pre-historic times? This fictional story proves that true love can overcome all differences. It was emotional and all kinds of beautiful.<br><br>And a little note/fact/warning about this book so it does not catch you unprepared. Taking into consideration that we are talking about <b>pre-historic times</b> in this book, there is visible lack of real dialogues, conversations or direct speech. But believe me, it does not reduce the captivity of this novel. On contrary, it makes it even more special and unique!<br><br><i>*ARC provided by author as an exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3777936271812386355" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/835017337" />
    <a title="Claire Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson"><img alt="Claire Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431471072p2/14026987.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/835017337?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claire Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claire Robinson" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson">Claire Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14026987-claire-robinson?shelf=books-i-cannot-live-without">books-i-cannot-live-without</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer835017337" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5474549557025582852"><b>ITS LIVE....IF YOU BUY ONE BOOK THIS YEAR IT NEEDS TO BE THIS ONE!.</b><br/><br/>I want to give this book more than 5 stars, it's just that good.<br/><br/><b>I will provide for her. I will protect her. I will give her anything she wants.</b><br/><br/>Transcendence is quite simply perfection, and right now, I want to rewind my life back to when I began reading it, when my expectations were at a manageable level, and my interest was mainly piqued because of an unusual synopsis, with it being very different to the books I have generally r</span>
  <span id="freeText5474549557025582852" style="display:none"><b>ITS LIVE....IF YOU BUY ONE BOOK THIS YEAR IT NEEDS TO BE THIS ONE!.</b><br /><br />I want to give this book more than 5 stars, it's just that good.<br /><br /><b>I will provide for her. I will protect her. I will give her anything she wants.</b><br /><br />Transcendence is quite simply perfection, and right now, I want to rewind my life back to when I began reading it, when my expectations were at a manageable level, and my interest was mainly piqued because of an unusual synopsis, with it being very different to the books I have generally read of late. Now that I have finished it, I can without a doubt say it has ruined me. I know it is unlikely that I will have to opportunity to read something as well crafted, beautifully executed and un-put-down-able for a long time to come. <br /><br />I am 100% in love with this book. Every. Thing. About. It.<br /><br />I think the genius behind Shay’s writing, and my total awe for her stems from the fact that the book is told completely from Ehd’s point of view. As you would expect from a caveman there is virtually no vocalization or conversation between him and Elizabeth (Beh) and although I would love to tell you the words that they do use to communicate with each other I am not going too, because they would give far too much away, but just thinking about it makes me smile!<br /><br /><b>She is enough to warm me – inside and out.</b><br /><br />There are so many parts of this book that I want to comment on, but seeing as I am someone who only offers spoiler-free reviews it is difficult to put anything down, without giving too much away. I do have a list of things that stand out as hands down, some of my favourites though –<br /><br />•	Bath-times<br />•	Hair-brushing &amp; detangling<br />•	P.M.T<br />•	Nose Nuzzling<br />•	Hand Holding<br />•	Shaving<br />•	Pillows<br />•	Pottery<br /><br />All quite inane things but put together in Transcendence, just out and out awesome!<br /><br /><b>She is everything to me, and I have to be a good mate to her.</b><br /><br />Who knew how easy it would be too fall in love with a caveman... well I have wholeheartedly and irrevocably. My only disappointment is that I cannot comprehensively write a review that does the book the true justice it deserves, or emphasizes just how stunningly beautiful, and wholly unforgettable that it is.<br /><br /><b>I will never, ever hurt my Beh.</b><br /><br />ARC provided by the author, and I cannot express my gratitude for the opportunity to read and review what will now be without doubt one of my all-time favourite books.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5474549557025582852" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen " href="/user/show/5962787-jen">Jen </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=over-the-top-sweet">over-the-top-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=head-trippin">head-trippin</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1389590407" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17453027879703177905"><b>5 Hoh! Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>My life with Beh was beautiful, transcending everything that set us apart from each other and bringing us together with our family and tribe.</i>
</b><br/><br/>What a truly beautiful and unique love story! I knew at some point I'd get around to reading this simply because the premise was too different for me to ignore, but the idea of the story narrated solely from the POV of a prehistoric dude had me doubting how much I'd enjoy it. <br/><br/>To be fair I don't REALLY know That much about the prehistoric-ish</span>
  <span id="freeText17453027879703177905" style="display:none"><b>5 Hoh! Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>My life with Beh was beautiful, transcending everything that set us apart from each other and bringing us together with our family and tribe.</i>
</b><br><br>What a truly beautiful and unique love story! I knew at some point I'd get around to reading this simply because the premise was too different for me to ignore, but the idea of the story narrated solely from the POV of a prehistoric dude had me doubting how much I'd enjoy it. <br><br>To be fair I don't REALLY know That much about the prehistoric-ish era. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455512430i/18110741.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, that's not entirely true but it's close. So sue me.<br><br>Imagine my surprise when I was sucked into this book from the first few pages.<br><br>I didn't expect to relate to Ehd, but as the story rolled on it became evident that his needs weren't a whole lot different than that of Beh, his eventual mate and love. And I have to say picturing Ehd and Beh both becoming frustrated with the other and the communication difficulties brought a smile to my face more than once. <br><br><b>
  <i>Most of the noises she makes just hurt my head, but I don’t mind so much. She’s my mate, she’s unusual, and she is mine.</i>
</b><br><br>The fact that Ehd had to learn to endure Beh's chatty ways added to the overall delightfulness of this book. Yep, I said delightful. My husband had to learn to endure the same damn thing!<br><br><b>
  <i>When I put my penis inside of her, it feels too good to slow down. Besides, once I finish, I’m really tired, and all I want to do is lie down. If I make sure she feels good first, then she might let me sleep afterwards.</i>
</b><br><br>See? Some things are universal regardless of time and space.<br><br>I went back and forth between a 4 and 5 star rating but when it comes right down to it, I have to give some major props to Shay Savage for creating a truly unique love story. In a world of romance books filled with misunderstandings, jealous exes and non committal jackasses, <i>Transcendence</i> and its creativity stands alone.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17453027879703177905" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1080296685" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1080296685" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1080296685?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=love-this-author">love-this-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1080296685" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4772813967560835824"><b><br/>~Re-read with my girl Sue 5/6/2016~<br/><br/>This book is simply stunning! The re-read only made me fall more in love with Ehd. This love story is timeless and unforgettable!~<br/>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br/><br/>REVIEW POSTED 10/17/2014<br/>"I wrap my arms around her and twist our legs together as well, just for good measure. I want to make sure nothing can separate us. I want to be positive we will remain together forever."-Ehd </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413844508i/11571150.jpg' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Who knew I would be completely held captive by a book told in the male PO</span>
  <span id="freeText4772813967560835824" style="display:none"><b><br>~Re-read with my girl Sue 5/6/2016~<br><br>This book is simply stunning! The re-read only made me fall more in love with Ehd. This love story is timeless and unforgettable!~<br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>REVIEW POSTED 10/17/2014<br>"I wrap my arms around her and twist our legs together as well, just for good measure. I want to make sure nothing can separate us. I want to be positive we will remain together forever."-Ehd </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413844508i/11571150.jpg" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Who knew I would be completely held captive by a book told in the male POV, with only a few words of dialogue, and set back in the caveman days? Transcendence is possibly one of the most tender well written books of all time. <br><br>Ehd is all alone. His tribe has been killed and he has been surviving. He isn't really living. He longs for a companion. He longs to have a family. He wants to have a tribe. As he is out on a hunt, he stumbles across a horrible sound....a girl screaming.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413844508i/11571151.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beh is scared and alone. Ehd scoops her up and brings her back to his pad (aka cave!)<br><br><b>"She is so beautiful—her smooth hair and her deep eyes and her creamy, pale skin. I don’t like the noises she makes, but she looks to be able enough, even if she is small. I briefly wonder if she is fertile and if she would bear a child who looks like me. I like this idea. A lot. Finally, after all this time alone, I have a mate." </b><br><br>At first, Beh is terrified, scared, and continues to make sounds which annoy Ehd. He doesn't understand her. Still he does everything he can to provide for her and show her he is worthy of her. <br><br><b>"I will provide for her. I will protect her. I will give her anything she wants."</b><br><br>Beh slowly warms up to Ehd and tries to communicate with him. The form a friendship. Ehd still has it in his mind to mate with Beh as soon as possible. Beh is more hesitant. A great deal of time passes when finally Beh and Ehd kiss. It is so sweet and sexy all at the same time!<br><br><b>"The warmth of my mate’s mouth covers mine, and it sends tingles of sensation through the rest of my body as her tongue traces over my lower lip. The game that annoyed me in the beginning is now my favorite thing to do." </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413844508i/11571152._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Even as these two make a way to connect, Beh is still so strange to Ehd. He cannot understand her need to be clean, constant noise making, and her inability to do simple tasks that every woman should know how to do. This element of uncertainty continues to add humor and simplicity to the story. You just want to know what is going to happen next between these two! <br><br><b>"My mate is quite serious about this bathing thing. I don’t like it. Not at all." </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413844508i/11571153._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And did I mention the humor?<br><br><b>"Her mouth noises are almost constant, but so is her desire to pull me down into the furs and put me inside of her, and she has been like that for days and days. At first, I was thrilled. Now , I am completely worn out."</b><br><br>This story was just beautiful. The text is full of rich description. The emotions are deep. Ehd and Beh have to survive some very dangerous elements. They face great loss and great joy. The most thrilling about this read is that you want to know where Beh came from. What is happening? Will they be able to stay together? Will Beh find her way home and leave Ehd? I felt such a wave of emotions throughout this read. I was laughing, crying, and even blushing at times. Such a tender read with so much heart! This is a book that I will never forget! If you haven't read this book, drop everything and read it now! I know I will be rereading this one again soon! I KHIZZ LUFFS Ehd and Beh!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413845777i/11571450._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I have lived on my own for a long, long time, and just the last few seasons with Beh make me realize there is no way I ever want to be alone again. I would never be able to survive without Beh with me. I wouldn’t even want to live if she were no longer here." </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4772813967560835824" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/833052888?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833052888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17519652927122208463"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Transcendence<br/><b>Series:</b> Standalone (for now)<br/><b>Author:</b> Shay Savage<br/><b>Release Date: </b> February 14th , 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 2 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Shay Savage caught my attention with incredible as well as a little bit unbelievable idea, that totally did persuade me into reading Transcendence. I just couldn’t pass the opportunity to get my hands on a book about real caveman, could I? After reading so many delicious novels with alpha males aka modern cavemen, not diggi</span>
  <span id="freeText17519652927122208463" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Transcendence<br><b>Series:</b> Standalone (for now)<br><b>Author:</b> Shay Savage<br><b>Release Date: </b> February 14th , 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 2 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Shay Savage caught my attention with incredible as well as a little bit unbelievable idea, that totally did persuade me into reading Transcendence. I just couldn’t pass the opportunity to get my hands on a book about real caveman, could I? After reading so many delicious novels with alpha males aka modern cavemen, not digging into a book with a real one was for me almost a crime. <br><br>Not only did I was thrilled to find out exactly how this crazy story would go but I wanted and expected real alpha that would make my panties wet, my ovaries insane and just change into blubbery mess. I didn’t get that.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392543332i/8575918.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, I thought this story will go in completely different direction! I thought our caveman will be homo sapiens not complete primitive. In my mind, I saw this story as a spellbinding romance between modern woman and a man that lived in the wilderness, like Tarzan perhaps? Still caveman but intelligent, up – to – date human. <br><br>I’m sorry, but as captivating and original as the idea was, Transcendence is not a real romance in my eyes and it certainly didn’t make me swoon, laugh or have fun. For most of the time I was bored. Bored to tears. <br><br>I won’t be even telling you what the story is about, because frankly I could summarize the entire plot in few sentences. Reading the official blurb is as detailed as you could get. Mostly, Edh wanted to make his mate happy – give her water, food, nice cave to live in and baby. In his mind everything was about making babies. So we kind of get horny caveman and that’s all. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392543332i/8575919.jpg" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Reading only internal monologue of a prehistoric human, as there wasn’t any conversation, was boring. BORING. Yes, you guessed right Edh wasn’t very complex character. He was as simple as a man can get. I was turned off by this lack of conversations or at least some understanding between main characters. Edh was not able to comprehend and learn Elizabeth’s language at all. The only words he could use was his and Elizabeth name-sound (Edh and Beh), no, kiss and love. Nothing more. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392543332i/8575920.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Savage done a great job in psychological field of the story, though – I will admit that. I want to congratulate her for being so wonderful and detailed in telling a story from perspective of primitive man. Everything what made Edh a prehistoric human was perfectly thorough and comprehensive. Basic needs as food, water, shelter, safety and an heir were everything for him. But it didn’t make the story. Not for me. <br><br>In nutshell, I was pretty disappointed. Transcendence with it’s absolutely mind-blowing storyline should be the hit! Instead it was very slow-paced, meek and plain. <br><br><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img <div id="review_833601913" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/833601913" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/833601913?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833601913" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2882666868911828129"><b>Re-read November 27th 2018 and loved it all over again!<br/><br/>Transcendence</b> was amazing and I kept thinking about it for days after finishing. It was an original story about survival and finding a love that “transcendences” time.<br/><br/>Ehd is a caveman alone and barely getting by. He has his own little cave and should be out preparing for the coming winter, but with being so lonely, he can’t quite muster up the will to get to it. This all changes when he discovers a girl, Elizabeth or “Beh” as he calls her, s</span>
  <span id="freeText2882666868911828129" style="display:none"><b>Re-read November 27th 2018 and loved it all over again!<br /><br />Transcendence</b> was amazing and I kept thinking about it for days after finishing. It was an original story about survival and finding a love that “transcendences” time.<br /><br />Ehd is a caveman alone and barely getting by. He has his own little cave and should be out preparing for the coming winter, but with being so lonely, he can’t quite muster up the will to get to it. This all changes when he discovers a girl, Elizabeth or “Beh” as he calls her, stuck at the bottom of his animal trap. She is different from any other girl he’s come across. Beh wears strange coverings, and babbles on and on. But she’s another person and a female at that, and Ehd is overjoyed to have found her. He knows immediately that Beh must be his mate, and he sets out to convince her. Funnily enough, Beh has different ideas and so winning her over isn’t as easy as Ehd thought. <br /><br />This story is told through Ehd’s POV alone, and there is VERY little dialogue throughout, yet I loved being inside his head. Being a caveman, his goals and drive is very primal: food, shelter and mating to form his own tribe. But Ehd has profound emotions and a desire for love and acceptance that comes through loud and clear through his narrative. Ehd is so very grateful to have found Beh, and he puts her happiness and welfare far above his own. <br /><b><br />It is far beyond not wanting to be alone anymore. I want her—only her. I will do anything to make Beh mine.<br /><br />There is nothing more important than Beh, and if making her happy means my own sorrow, I will have to accept that.</b><br /><br />I couldn’t help but fall hard and fast for this caveman! I was so touched by Ehd’s kind and tender soul, and I hoped desperately he’d get his heart’s desire. <br /><br />This story was fascinating! From their struggles to survive, and the dangers that came along with it to the progressive deepening of both Beh and Ehd’s feelings for each other, I couldn’t put this book down. Oh my heart! <br /><br />I don’t want to say too much because I think it’s best to go into this story knowing as little as possible. I will say this is one of my favorite reads so far of 2014. I’ve read several books by Shay Savage, and her writing continues to amaze and impress me!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2882666868911828129" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1564510012" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1564510012" />
    <a title="Alp" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26653561-alp"><img alt="Alp" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1462791280p2/26653561.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1564510012?book_show_action=true">Feb 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alp" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alp" href="/user/show/26653561-alp">Alp</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=tearjerker">tearjerker</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1564510012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16331145413855326750">OH. MY. GOD. I’m a puddle of feels!<br/><br/>This book was so beautiful. I loved it. Absolutely loved it! I can’t believe it took me so long to pick up this one! Ehd and Beh’s story touched my heart in every way. Despite my high expectations, I never expected Transcendence to literally blow my mind like this. It was such a wonderful story, so much so that it kept me glued to the pages until the end. I’ve officially become Shay Savage’s fan.<br/><br/>This is exactly what happened to me while I was reading this book—</span>
  <span id="freeText16331145413855326750" style="display:none">OH. MY. GOD. I’m a puddle of feels!<br /><br />This book was so beautiful. I loved it. Absolutely loved it! I can’t believe it took me so long to pick up this one! Ehd and Beh’s story touched my heart in every way. Despite my high expectations, I never expected Transcendence to literally blow my mind like this. It was such a wonderful story, so much so that it kept me glued to the pages until the end. I’ve officially become Shay Savage’s fan.<br /><br />This is exactly what happened to me while I was reading this book—I felt so alive, happy, but sad at times. I smiled. I laughed. I hoped. I feared. I cried. The story itself was so sweet, emotional, and hilarious all at once. Reading this book was like taking a journey through both good and bad times with Ehd and Beh, which I loved every minute I spent with them.<br /><br />I always have a soft corner in my heart for naïve heroes, and Ehd, as a character, thoroughly won me over! He’s so adorable, caring, protective, and most of all, he loved Beh wholeheartedly no matter how strange she was!<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>My mate is unusual, and I couldn’t be happier about it.<br /><br />I don’t care if she ever makes a basket that can hold grain, but I want her to be here with me. I want her to be close to me as I work or fish, and I want her to lie next to me in the furs at night. In my mind, she is with me always and forever.<br /><br />As long as she lets me hold her close to my chest, protect her, and keep her warm, everything will be all right.<br />With her, I feel complete and content.</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />*Sigh*<br /><br />Near the end of the book when Beh was so ill, Ehd took her to their first cave. Both of them knew this was their last JOURNEY and they were ready to go through this together.<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>I think of the first day I saw her, sitting at the bottom of my hunting pit. I remember how obstinate she was at first, though when I think back on it now, I realize she was only confused and frightened. I remember when she first untangled my hair for me and the little wooden carving I had made to help with the task.<br /><br />I remember the first time I was inside of Beh, touching the soft skin of her back as waves of pleasure moved over me. I remember when I placed my hand on her belly and felt Lah kick. I remember when Kay was born and how Lee helped me cut the cord and place his new sister on his mother’s stomach.<br /><br />I remember it all.</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />This was heartbreaking, yet so beautiful at the same time…<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Beh…loves…Ehd,” she whispers, and her eyes sparkle at me just like they did the first time I tried to put a baby inside of her. It seems so long ago, but also so recent, as if time isn’t really relevant to the feelings inside of us both.<br />But time still moves, and there is nothing I can do to stop it.<br />“Luffs Beh,” my mouth utters, and I am rewarded with her quiet smile and the touch of her thin fingers on my cheek. “Ehd luffs Beh.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />Oh my, this totally made me burst into tears! Broke my heart into tiny pieces! I cried my heart out for him… I can’t put my feelings into words… I just don’t know how to describe them here…<br /><br />By the way, this book left me emotionally overwhelmed. I not only enjoyed reading it but also loved every page I turned and every line I read. This is definitely one of my most memorable reading experiences, one of the best books of all time!<br /><br /><br />-----------------------------------<br /><br /><br />**Thanks for the buddy read, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26693609-ally-georgie" rel="nofollow noopener">Ally</a>!<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1838178429" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1838178429" />
    <a title="KAS" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20691061-kas"><img alt="KAS" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1472348331p2/20691061.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1838178429?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KAS" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KAS" href="/user/show/20691061-kas">KAS</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20691061-kas?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1838178429" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9772360242539312273">WHERE ON EARTH DO I BEGIN? I do not want to ruin the experience, except to tell you to expect the unexpected! It was beautiful. It was thoughtful. It was remarkable.<br/><br/>Months ago, I remember seeing the title of this book and the 5 star ratings pop up on the Goodreads feed, but I never read the reviews. I decided at some point I would read it based on the ratings and because the cover totally intrigued me. Since I was "going in blind" and unfamiliar with this author, I concocted scenarios in my mind</span>
  <span id="freeText9772360242539312273" style="display:none">WHERE ON EARTH DO I BEGIN? I do not want to ruin the experience, except to tell you to expect the unexpected! It was beautiful. It was thoughtful. It was remarkable.<br /><br />Months ago, I remember seeing the title of this book and the 5 star ratings pop up on the Goodreads feed, but I never read the reviews. I decided at some point I would read it based on the ratings and because the cover totally intrigued me. Since I was "going in blind" and unfamiliar with this author, I concocted scenarios in my mind of what I was about to read. Well .......<br /><br />Silly, silly woman! My scenarios couldn't have been more off the mark, and thank goodness for that. While reading, my emotions and anxiety levels were all over the place. I am so glad I did not read the blurb or reviews beforehand. I just dove in and let the pages speak for themselves! <br /><br />To me this was a slow burn, angst filled romance, which I could not get enough of.<br /><br />My friend, Carol [Goodreads Addict], said it best when she commented on my status update, "This book slayed me." <br /><br />I encourage you not to read reviews or the synopsis, but jump in feet first and prepare to be "slayed" ;)<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9772360242539312273" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_879578414" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/879578414" />
    <a title="Shelly Strange" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange"><img alt="Shelly Strange" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600285315p2/25393430.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/879578414?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Strange" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Strange" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange">Shelly Strange</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-romance">fantasy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=this-book-is-everything">this-book-is-everything</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=i-love-peer-pressure">i-love-peer-pressure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=dis-is-a-rully-good-lurv-story">dis-is-a-rully-good-lurv-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=your-argument-is-invalid">your-argument-is-invalid</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer879578414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7772702384502490839"><b>WARNING: May induce severe ugly crying.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443209061ra/16333211.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Wow. This book. Talk about a surprise. I was enjoying the story, but not loving it, up until about the 70% mark and then it just suddenly became this incredibly rich and emotional story that caused me to literally sob. I had to stop at 95% and wait to finish it when I could compose myself enough to carry on. This has never happened to me before when reading a book. (Yeah, there are several movies I have privately ugly-cried to – like The Notebook, Les Miser</span>
  <span id="freeText7772702384502490839" style="display:none"><b>WARNING: May induce severe ugly crying.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443209061ra/16333211.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow. This book. Talk about a surprise. I was enjoying the story, but not loving it, up until about the 70% mark and then it just suddenly became this incredibly rich and emotional story that caused me to literally sob. I had to stop at 95% and wait to finish it when I could compose myself enough to carry on. This has never happened to me before when reading a book. (Yeah, there are several movies I have privately ugly-cried to – like The Notebook, Les Miserables, when I saw Beaches for the first time…typical stuff like that.) <br><br>Some people will try to read this book and be baffled by the 5 star reviews. This is not for everyone. First off, not a lot happens until the book is more than halfway over! This is not going to work for people who need a lot going on in the plot. It’s written in a very simple style and ALL about the slow-evolving romance. The male main character is not an alpha at all. <b>
  <u>He’s a caveman.</u>
</b> He does not have the capacity to learn language or symbols or understand them because his brain is different from modern humans. So there is repetition and not a lot of complexity going on. Ehd is a simple man. He wants a mate. He wants to protect and provide for his mate. And he REALLY wants to “put a baby” inside his mate. All the time.<br><br>There are a zillion reviews for this, so I won’t recap or include quotes. The basic premise is that a caveman stumbles upon a strange woman and decides she is his mate. As the reader, we learn that his mate, Beh (he can’t pronounce her real name, Elizabeth), somehow came from another time and is trapped there. As the story unfolds, they fall in love, and have a long, fulfilling life together. <br><br>The author did an amazing job in telling this story completely from Ehd’s point of view. Of course, it is not “realistic” because Ehd thinks in a more complex way than a caveman would. But there would be no story if the author didn’t take some artistic liberties. I’ve never read a book like this and it’s very original.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443209061ra/16333212.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was not prepared for how emotionally attached I would become to Ehd and Beh. It literally makes me tear up just thinking about it. Even halfway through the book, I did not feel very emotional one way or the other about it, and then it just snuck up on me, and BAM. I was viscerally involved. <br><br>Romances are hit and miss with me. Sometimes I loathe them and sometimes I enjoy them. Rarely, do I flat-out LOVE them. This one is now an all-time favorite.<br><br>Sometimes it’s nice to read a romance about a male that is not a “mega alpha.” Ehd loved Beh so much. At first, I was like, eh, I need my book men to be more dominant, I’m not sure about this… but it WORKED. Ehd is the male you’d want in real life. Not the snarky sexy controlling asshole that is so common in most romances. <br><br>Well, I guess I will wrap it up. If you like sweet romances with a little bit of fantasy thrown in, one that is about the slow relationship build and kind of simple, yet invokes strong emotions, you will no doubt love this. <b>
  <u>You’ll love it.</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443209061ra/16333213.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>^^^ That gif pretty much sums up the theme of this story.<br><br>Anyway, highly recommended for romance fans. I’ll shut up now.<br><br><b>Buddy Read with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-another-buddy-read" rel="nofollow noopener">MacHalo group</a>, starting September 23, 2015. Because caveman romance, duh. For research purposes.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438614332i/15734858.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7772702384502490839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833930076" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6184937302130396650"><b>4 Caveman Style Stars<br/><br/><i>Ehd luffs Beh</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394090512ra/8806702.gif' width='400' height='180' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>When a man without a tribe find his mate at the bottom of his hunting pit, the real love adventure begins....</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394090512i/8806703.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You think you 've met the ultimate alpha male?<br/>You think you know what goes on inside his head?<br/>You think you have trouble communicating with you man?<br/><br/><pre>THINK AGAIN!</pre><br/><br/>Ehd is a real, living and breathing caveman that the mate he was always expecting falls literally in his lap, or his pit but you catch my drift. She is not at all what he had in mind. She makes a l</span>
  <span id="freeText6184937302130396650" style="display:none"><b>4 Caveman Style Stars<br><br><i>Ehd luffs Beh</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394090512ra/8806702.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>When a man without a tribe find his mate at the bottom of his hunting pit, the real love adventure begins....</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394090512i/8806703.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You think you 've met the ultimate alpha male?<br>You think you know what goes on inside his head?<br>You think you have trouble communicating with you man?<br><br><pre>THINK AGAIN!</pre><br><br>Ehd is a real, living and breathing caveman that the mate he was always expecting falls literally in his lap, or his pit but you catch my drift. She is not at all what he had in mind. She makes a lot of sounds that make his head ache, she likes everything clean, she cries and the worst of all? Will she let him put a baby inside her and make everything right in his world?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394090512i/8806704._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394090512i/8806705._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Entirely in Ehd's POV we witness the struggles, love and survival story of a prehistoric man and a modern woman. Ehd's inner monologue is endearing and touching as the unsuspecting and clueless man has to deal with his urges, his headstrong woman, provide and protect the one he claimed. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394090639i/8806708.png" width="400" height="267" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unusual, unconventional and despite the lack of dialogues, emotional, this is a beautiful love story and I have to congratulate <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5160667.Shay_Savage" title="Shay Savage" rel="nofollow noopener">Shay Savage</a>, for managing to pull it off. It is something different than the usual romances, endearing, sweet and sexy at the same time. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386398490ra/7356289.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It will stay with me, and I will always remember Ehd and his Beh. Or Elizabeth if you have a functioning Broca Area... ;)<br><br><br><i>Pre-release excitement</i><br><b>TEAM CAVEMAN!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385690811i/7202333.gif" width="400" height="295" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Can't wait...</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390654855ra/8257914.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_833226170" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/833226170" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/833226170?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833226170" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16185308763395860690"><b>The <i>original</i> alpha....</b><br/><br/>It's no surprise that I was immediately drawn to this book due to the unusual nature of the synopsis. A synopsis that immediately made me stop and stare. Stare and contemplate. <i>How in the hell is Shay Savage going to pull this off?</i> Can it be pulled off? Curiosity....piqued.<br/><br/>Curiosity is what drove me to read <i>Transcendence</i>. Curiosity and a craving for something original. Originality is what stole my heart. <br/><br/>Ingeniously written, and creatively done. I. Was. Impressed. <br/><br/>Shay Sava</span>
  <span id="freeText16185308763395860690" style="display:none"><b>The <i>original</i> alpha....</b><br /><br />It's no surprise that I was immediately drawn to this book due to the unusual nature of the synopsis. A synopsis that immediately made me stop and stare. Stare and contemplate. <i>How in the hell is Shay Savage going to pull this off?</i> Can it be pulled off? Curiosity....piqued.<br /><br />Curiosity is what drove me to read <i>Transcendence</i>. Curiosity and a craving for something original. Originality is what stole my heart. <br /><br />Ingeniously written, and creatively done. I. Was. Impressed. <br /><br />Shay Savage not only delivered a heart dropping romance, but managed to develop two characters from one POV. Doing this, without words!! Without conversation. All from the eyes and thoughts of a caveman. And it worked. It was perfect. <br /><br />At first, I was a little put off by some of the phrase repetition. Yes, I get that Ehd thinks his "mate is strange" and sex is synonymous for "put a baby in her", but must he say this over and over...and over again? The answer....YES! I had to remind myself that he <i>is</i> a caveman, simple. Did I really expect him to say, "Damn that b**ch is weird" or "Maybe tonight she'll let me f**k her from behind." His words are <i>his</i> words, and I learned acceptance. He <i>earned</i> acceptance!<br /><br />That acceptance was earned because of the captivating evolution of Ehd. The simplicity of a man that evolved emotionally, sexually. You wholefully experience the growth and development of a person, a relationship, and ultimately an epic love. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>I look down at her closely, making sure she is not actually hurt, and run my nose over hers so she knows I will care for her. I'm tired and my muscles are sore, but Beh comes first.</b>
</i><br /><br />His devotion and duty was undeniably arousing, but when you see that devotion transcend into love your emotions become overwhelmed. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>Despite her oddities, she is without a doubt perfect in every way that matters to me.</b>
</i><br /><br />I'll admit that close to midway, the pace faltered briefly and I became a little impatient, but it picked up and the story seemed to come alive again. I was also left with some unanswered questions, a few points of confusion, and felt the ending transpired a little too quickly. But at the same time, the rapid passage of time allowed us <i>more</i> time with Beh and Ehd. I'm also a little indifferent about the explanation of Beh, but I guess she had to come from somewhere.<br /><br />Just thinking back on this book though, so many things put a smile on my face and flood my heart with emotion. I giggle every time I think of "Hoh" and still laugh non stop at...<br /><br /><b><i>It's big, but it's not</i> that<i> big.</i></b><br /><br /><i>
  <b>I can't put a baby in there!</b>
</i><br /><br />My heart aches just thinking about the epilogue. It brought me to the realization of how much these characters actually touched me. How their love invaded my heart. All this, because Shay Savage allowed me to become part of their world. Part of their love, and their love...<br /><br />Their love was transcendent! <br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br />More reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16185308763395860690" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_871076356" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/871076356" />
    <a title="Shurrn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn"><img alt="Shurrn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410564134p2/22115857.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/871076356?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer871076356" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6391558043731575742"><b>It's official: I've fallen in love with a caveman...</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385263421ra/7112064.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>My life with Beh was beautiful, transcending everything that set us apart from each other.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> It's hard to write a review when you're absolutely blown away... and that is precisely what has happened with this book...<br/><br/><u>Before I started reading Transcendence, I believed the following:</u><br/>I thought it was impossible to have a full length novel where there are less than six words of dialogue spoken between the characters.<br/><br/>IF you managed to write</span>
  <span id="freeText6391558043731575742" style="display:none"><b>It's official: I've fallen in love with a caveman...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385263421ra/7112064.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>My life with Beh was beautiful, transcending everything that set us apart from each other.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> It's hard to write a review when you're absolutely blown away... and that is precisely what has happened with this book...<br><br><u>Before I started reading Transcendence, I believed the following:</u><br>I thought it was impossible to have a full length novel where there are less than six words of dialogue spoken between the characters.<br><br>IF you managed to write a novel after accomplishing such an unbelievable feat, I would have told you there was no way I would believe a <b>love story</b> could flourish between to characters who said less than half a dozen words to each other... <br><br>Or at least not a <i>believable</i> love story...<br><br>I would have been wrong.<br>So, so wrong...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397257ra/766355.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Is there anything Shay Savage <i>can't</i> do?<br>I can hardly believe that I have to add a CAVEMAN to my harem of Book Boyfriends, but I do...<br><br><b>EHD</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402865549i/10001237._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>In my mind, she is with me always and forever.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Ehd is a caveman - not the metaphorical Neanderthal alpha-male, he's <i>literally</i> a caveman. He lives in a cave, forages, and hunts with a spear. He lost his tribe and now lives completely alone. The entire story is told from his perspective and his primitive understanding of situations is often humorous, and always entertaining. One day while hunting, he comes across a hysterical female...<br><br><b>BEH</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402865549i/10001238._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She is so beautiful - her smooth hair and her deep eyes and her creamy, pale skin. I don't like the noises she makes, but she looks to be able enough, even if she is small. I briefly wonder is she is fertile and if she would bear a child who looks like me.<br>I like this idea.<br>A lot.<br>Finally, after all this time alone, I have a mate.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> We're able to glean from Ehd's limited understanding of the universe, that Elizabeth ("Beh" to Ehd's primitive language skills) does not belong in this time period. She is a contemporary woman who suddenly appears in a caveman's pit trap...<br><br>This book was un-put-down-able perfection and I loved every unique moment of it.<br>I laughed, I cried, I swooned... I wound up with a massive book hangover which could only be cured by peach margaritas.<br>Don't judge ;)<br>This is the kind of book I can read over and over again...<br><br><b>I had the opportunity to chat with Shay Savage at the 2014 louisville Author Event.<br>She's not only a talented author, she's also a fabulous person to talk to. Also... She &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4831114.C_L__Parker" title="C.L. Parker" rel="nofollow noopener">C.L. Parker</a> got a bit drunk which was endlessly entertaining!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396733022i/9179729._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396733023i/9179730._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6391558043731575742" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2632458110" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2632458110" />
    <a title="peachygirl" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/51435362-peachygirl"><img alt="peachygirl" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555561561p2/51435362.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2632458110?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="peachygirl" class="user" itemprop="url" name="peachygirl" href="/user/show/51435362-peachygirl">peachygirl</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/51435362-peachygirl?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2632458110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1941921967009760558">Safe to say I've never read anything like this before. Ehd and Elizabeth's story was truly one of a kind! <br/><br/>For a human like primate aka Homo savage (the writer's words, not mine), Ehd is surprisingly gentle. And kinda adorable. I loved seeing everything through his eyes, inspite of the lack of conversation. It did take me a while to get used to the narrative, since he rarely thinks about anything other than "putting a baby" in his mate, but I was astonished by how tender hearted he really was. To</span>
  <span id="freeText1941921967009760558" style="display:none">Safe to say I've never read anything like this before. Ehd and Elizabeth's story was truly one of a kind! <br /><br />For a human like primate aka Homo savage (the writer's words, not mine), Ehd is surprisingly gentle. And kinda adorable. I loved seeing everything through his eyes, inspite of the lack of conversation. It did take me a while to get used to the narrative, since he rarely thinks about anything other than "putting a baby" in his mate, but I was astonished by how tender hearted he really was. To the point where he was willing to do anything to keep his mate safe. What a precious sweetheart!<br />His Beh was equally wonderful. <br /><br />The writer does take a lot of liberties with her "artistic license", but it was such a beautiful read that I ignored most of the inaccuracies. And the epilogue cleared up some of the doubts I had. <br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed reading about Ehd, the way his mind works, his interaction with Beh and their kids, his endearing nose rubs and even his and Beh's physical relationship. Rather than being smutty, I found it really cute. Every time he made the sounds of 'khzz' or 'luffs' to make Beh smile, a part of me melted. And the last chapter was beautiful beyond words. <br />4.5 'luffly' stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1941921967009760558" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('q4VDV6b+t42Um1LrUExriyw4s23y2JUlr6k72lKpgyqRoyqFHaB+5TOw5oqnuWFU+mdUpTxVG0L0131rn+pxsA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6611687862292289707">Shay Savage is an independent author from Cincinnati, Ohio, where she lives with her family and a variety of household pets. She is an accomplished public speaker and holds the rank of Distinguished Toastmaster from Toastmasters International. Her hobbies include off-roading in her big, yellow Jeep, science fiction in all forms, and soccer. Savage holds a degree in psychology, and she brings a lot</span>
  <span id="freeText6611687862292289707" style="display:none">Shay Savage is an independent author from Cincinnati, Ohio, where she lives with her family and a variety of household pets. She is an accomplished public speaker and holds the rank of Distinguished Toastmaster from Toastmasters International. Her hobbies include off-roading in her big, yellow Jeep, science fiction in all forms, and soccer. Savage holds a degree in psychology, and she brings a lot of that knowledge into the characters within her stories.<br /><br />From the author: “It’s my job to make you FEEL. That doesn’t always mean you’ll feel good, but I want my readers to be connected enough to my characters to care.”<br /><br />Savage’s books many books span a wide variety of topics and sub-genres with deeply flawed characters. From cavemen to addicts to hitmen, you’ll find yourself falling for these seemingly irredeemable characters!<br /><br /></span>
